[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run against the Apache Commons Compress `Expander` example [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered a critical security exception. The sanitizer detected a file path [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal when expanding archive entries, as the code accepted a path containing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“..” segments and attempted to write outside the intended extraction directory.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  A `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` was raised by the Jazzer sanitizer for **file [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath traversal**.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer provided an input that led `Expander.expand` to process a path with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded “..[0m[35m/[0m[95m..[0m[39m” sequences.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The Jazzer `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer hook [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`pathFirstArgHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intercepted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe file access.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. In `FilePathTraversal.check`, the sanitized path [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m…[0m[35m/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` was flagged as traversing above[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe designated boundary.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The exception stack trace shows the flow through multiple overloads of [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.expand`, culminating in the sanitizer check in `FilePathTraversal`.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The vulnerability arises during archive extraction when entry names are not [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfully normalized before file creation.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal`, indicating that the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer’s path checks are functioning as intended by blocking unsafe writes.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply drives the `Expander` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI; it is not the root cause but the entry point for triggering the issue.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The repeated calls to `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m suggest a recursive or iterative extraction process where path [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitization may be bypassed or insufficient.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **FilePathTraversal** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Methods: `check`, `checkPath`, `pathFirstArgHook`  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **Expander** [0m[1;39m([0m[39morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Overloaded `expand` methods at the locations noted in the stack trace  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Entry-name normalization and output-path resolution logic  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • **Fuzzer harness** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Invocation of the `expand` API, input handling, and temporary directory setup[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA holistic review should focus on how archive entry names are sanitized or [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcanonicalized before file I/O, ensuring that directory traversal sequences cannot [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape the intended extraction root.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn initial Jazzer fuzzing run against the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception complaining of a file [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Zip slip`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when expanding archives with entries containing “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences. To guard against such traversal, a patch was proposed that replaces the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal `resolveIn` implementation in `ArchiveEntry.java` with logic that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURL-decodes the entry name, normalizes the resulting path, and throws an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` if the normalized path does not remain under the intended output [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory. When the patch was applied and the project was rebuilt under Maven, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation failed with the error:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    variable decodedName might already have been assigned[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchi[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mveEntry.java[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m85[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m13[0m[1;39m][0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a problem in the new variable assignment logic.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A Jazzer sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected a file path traversal during[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing of the `Expander` example in Apache Commons Compress.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The exception trace shows that the sanitizer’s `pathFirstArgHook` was invoked [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `FilePathTraversal.checkPath`, triggered by calls to `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The offending archive entry path contained “..” segments that escaped the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory, leading to a security violation report from the fuzzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The default interface method `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` was [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original behavior:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Resolve the raw entry name against `parentPath`, normalize it, and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately throw on traversal.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Attempt to URL-decode the entry name in a secondary `try` block, falling [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback to the already-normalized path if decoding failed.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Patched behavior:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Introduce a local `decodedName` variable.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In a `try` block, assign `decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"US-ASCII"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In the corresponding `catch` block, fallback to `decodedName = name`.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Resolve and normalize `decodedName` against `parentPath`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Throw an `IOException` if the normalized result does not start with [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Return the normalized, checked path otherwise.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Build Log After Patch  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The project recompilation under Maven stopped with a single compilation error [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `ArchiveEntry.java`:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `variable decodedName might already have been assigned`  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This error indicates that the Java compiler sees an ambiguous or conflicting [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massignment to the local variable `decodedName` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmost likely due to the way it was [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclared `final` and assigned in both `try` and `catch`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The declaration and assignment of `decodedName` in [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`—verify that it is declared once and definitively assigned [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly once along every control flow path, without accidental redeclaration or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple assignment.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The remainder of the `resolveIn` method, including any leftover references to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe old `outputFile` variable or legacy code paths that may interact with [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m             if [1m([0m![1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                      parentPath, name, outputFile[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             return outputFile;                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ```                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patched code:                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ```                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         default Path [1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mfinal Path parentPath[1m)[0m throws IOException [1m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final String name = [1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final String decodedName;                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             try [1m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 decodedName = [1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname, [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m catch [1m([0mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[1m)[0m [1m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 [35m/[0m[35m/[0m Fallback to raw name if decoding fails                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 decodedName = name;                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             final Path resolved = [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             if [1m([0m![1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 throw new [1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                     [1;35mString.format[0m[1m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' -> '%s'"[0m, parentPath, decodedName[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             return resolved;                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ```                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A new variable `decodedName` is introduced to hold a URL-decoded version of the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive entry name [1m([0mor the raw name on failure[1m)[0m.                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The code now normalizes and checks the resolved path to prevent traversal.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Build Result After Patch                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The Maven compiler reports an error in `ArchiveEntry.java`:                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           variable decodedName might already have been assigned                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This error suggests that the Java compiler sees multiple assignment paths to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `decodedName` that are not mutually exclusive, likely due to mixing a `try…catch`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         assignment with a fallback assignment in the same scope.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Areas for Further Investigation                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **ArchiveEntry.resolveIn implementation**                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Review the variable scoping and assignments for `decodedName` to ensure it is  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         declared and assigned exactly once in all code paths.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Verify that imports [1m([0m`java.net.URLDecoder`,                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets`, `java.io.UnsupportedEncodingException`[1m)[0m are    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         correct and no name collisions exist.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Expander.expand usage**                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Examine how `resolveIn` is used in the `Expander` example to confirm that it   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         is invoked for every entry and that any additional sanitization [1m([0me.g., symbolic     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         link handling[1m)[0m is accounted for.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **FilePathTraversal sanitizer interaction**                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Understand how Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` hook interacts with Commons        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Compress internals. Investigate if path traversal checks in the library itself      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         happen before or after the sanitizer’s hook.                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **Other archive entry types**                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Check whether other archive formats or entry implementations bypass            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `resolveIn` or use alternative resolution logic that could reintroduce path         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal issues.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This evaluation report outlines the original fuzzer-detected path traversal, the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         user’s patch attempt and its compilation failure, and highlights code areas needing [2m                [0m
